11999,"""""""

import requests
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_data(url):
    r = requests.get(url).json()
    return r['hits']['hits']


def search_by_field(field, condition):
    url = 'http://localhost:9200/vaers-raw/_search'

    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""bool"": {
                ""must"": [{
                    ""match"": {
                        f""{field}"": f""{condition}""
                    }
                }]
            }
        },
        ""size"": 10000
    }

    res = es.search(index=""vaers-raw"", body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(DIED)s %(STATE)s"" % hit[""_source""])


if __name__"

4248,"{
    ""query"": {
        ""range"" : {
            ""RECVDATE"" : {
                ""gte"":""2021-03-01"",
                ""lte"":""2021-05-01"",
                ""format"":""yyyy-MM-dd||epoch_millis""
            }
        }
    }
}

""""""

def get_condition(field):
    if field == 'RECVDATE':
        return {'gte':'2021-03-01', 'lte':'2021-05-01','format':'yyyy-MM-dd||epoch_millis'}
    elif field == 'STATE':
        return ['VA']
    else:
        return None


def generate_elasticsearch_query(field, condition=None):
    if not condition:
        condition = get_condition(field)

    if isinstance(condition, list):
        return {""terms"":{field:condition}}"

def get_condition(field):

            }
        }}

    elif field == 'STATE':
        return {""term"":{""STATE"":""VA""}}

        return {""range"":{
            ""AGE_YRS"":{
                ""gte"":45"
